MERGE (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
SET item.level = 1,
    item.xp = 3,
    item.productionTime = "2 min",
    item.quantity = 1,
    item.imageUrl = "https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/hayday/images/e/e2/Wheat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20240218150024",
    item.minPrice = 50,
    item.maxPrice = 101;


MERGE (location:ProductionLocation {name: "Field"})
MERGE (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (item)-[:PRODUCED_IN]->(location);


MATCH (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MERGE (item:Item {name: "Mocha Milkshake"})
SET item.level = 125,
    item.xp = 856,
    item.productionTime = "30 min★★★ 25 min",
    item.quantity = 125,
    item.imageUrl = "data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D",
    item.minPrice = 1,
    item.maxPrice = 0;


MERGE (location:ProductionLocation {name: "Milkshake Bar"})
MERGE (item:Item {name: "Mocha Milkshake"})
MERGE (item)-[:PRODUCED_IN]->(location);


MATCH (item:Item {name: "Mocha Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Chocolate Ice Cream"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);


MATCH (item:Item {name: "Mocha Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Espresso"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 2}]->(ingredient);
